<div id="review_89894825" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/89894825" />
    <a title="Nic" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2813423-nic"><img alt="Nic" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/89894825?book_show_action=true">Feb 16, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nic" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nic" href="/user/show/2813423-nic">Nic</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780553820317" href="/book/show/7663247-succubus-shadows">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2813423-nic?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2813423-nic?shelf=2010">2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2813423-nic?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer89894825" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4691541907159180438">Richelle Mead is one of my favourite authors and this book did not disappoint. This book had it all. It was witty, humorous, had a great love story, action and twists and turns.<br/><br/>The writing in this book is fast paced so I easily read this within 24 hours. The character are well written and I love Georgina even more in this book. I found I liked Seth more as well than I have in the last couple which is good because I think he is going to play a major part in Georgina getting her happily ever after</span>
  <span id="freeText4691541907159180438" style="display:none">Richelle Mead is one of my favourite authors and this book did not disappoint. This book had it all. It was witty, humorous, had a great love story, action and twists and turns.<br /><br />The writing in this book is fast paced so I easily read this within 24 hours. The character are well written and I love Georgina even more in this book. I found I liked Seth more as well than I have in the last couple which is good because I think he is going to play a major part in Georgina getting her happily ever after ending. Their realitionship was quite emotional at times and you begin to think will Georgina ever catch a break and get what she wants.<br /><br />Overall if you like the Georgina Kincaid series you will love this book. If you are interesting in trying this series you'll have to start from the beginning but it is definelty worth it. <br /><br />I can't wait for the next book in the series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4691541907159180438" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer862688299" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13522691454184491491"><i>
  <b>Solid 4 Stars</b>
</i><br/><br/><i>Previously on <s>One Life to Live</s> uh..."One Soul to Steal" A.K.A The Georgina Kincaid Series.<br/><br/>Georgina lost her succubus powers and had an affair with Seth, betraying his girlfriend Maddie (who is still the most oblivious idiot I have ever seen, but I digress).<br/><br/>They break up again because what they did was wrong (duh!).<br/><br/>Seth overcompensates for his guilt and proposes to Maddie (craaaap, overkill much, dude).<br/><br/>However, because of his guilt, he now has a blight on his soul meaning that wh</i></span>
  <span id="freeText13522691454184491491" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>Solid 4 Stars</b>
</i><br><br><i>Previously on <s>One Life to Live</s> uh..."One Soul to Steal" A.K.A The Georgina Kincaid Series.<br><br>Georgina lost her succubus powers and had an affair with Seth, betraying his girlfriend Maddie (who is still the most oblivious idiot I have ever seen, but I digress).<br><br>They break up again because what they did was wrong (duh!).<br><br>Seth overcompensates for his guilt and proposes to Maddie (craaaap, overkill much, dude).<br><br>However, because of his guilt, he now has a blight on his soul meaning that when he dies, he's going straight to hell (harsh, but I'm okay with it, I'm still pissed at him for the whole Maddie thing, the idiot).<br><br>Roman is back; he helped rescue is father and is now Georgina's new roommate. Is there romance in the air?</i><br><br>And now the new episode of "One Soul to Steal":<br><br>Seth is getting married to Maddie, who asks Georgina for help planning and preparing for the wedding and to be her bridesmaid. Needless to say our succubus is fighting some serious depression. Meanwhile, another ex, this one actually tried to kill her once, Roman, is now her roommate and giving signals that he may still have feelings for Georgina. Meanwhile, Georgina has been having some sleepwalking episodes where she's being pulled/tempted towards something, and whatever supernatural creature this is, is praying on her when she's particularly down, not that hard to do considering she's always down lately with good reason. Eventually she gives in, and is taken, now it's everyone else that needs to find a way to rescue her. We also have a new succubus in town, Simone, that seems hell-bent (*snickers* get it) on corrupting our Seth(yes, I may be having a love/hate relationship with his guts right now but he's still ours, damn it; that bitch better calm the f*** down.)<br><br>SPOILER ALERT! MAJOR SPOILERS AHEAD!<br><br>What I loved most about this book is that this time, it was Georgina needing rescuing and not her to the rescue. We also find out everything about Georgina's past because the creature that have taken her are torturing with memories that are sometimes true, sometimes false, or sometimes both. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[To top it all off, Simone (the bitch) is impersonating Georgina in order to get Seth, but our boy doesn't fall for it thanks partly to our little Kayla, that sweet, sweet child. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. This book is basically about Georgina, her past loves, her past pain, what makes her who she is today. I loved it all and seeing what she's been through, I understand a lot more about her. <br><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The gang manages to save Georgina but with the help of Seth, who dropped everything to save her; however the fact that he managed to save her is a mystery in itself because it should have been impossible. Then, he finally breaks it off with Maddie, realizing that if he can't be with Georgina, he'd rather be alone. <br><br>Now to something I didn't see coming, paparazzi getting a picture of Seth with Georgina when she went to give him a Come to Jesus talk after the breakup, and she finds him at his most depressed and pessimistic, completely unrecognizable from our Seth of yesterbooks. At the end, the picture made everyone at the bookstore blame Georgina for the Seth/Maddie break up. While I'm sorry she was hurt, in all honesty, who gave a shit about Maddie anyway. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Now my message to the characters:<br>Georgina= my heart breaks for you but then again, my heart's always<br> breaking for you.<br>Seth= boy, you better get your shit together.<br>Roman= Are you seriously still trying to bang that drum? (quote <br> from new CW show Star-Crossed, it just tickled me.)<br>Jerome= you know something, don't you, you cold-hearted bastard.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393628531i/8742733.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Carter= you know I love you, and while the things you say are lovely, <br> they're not really helpful. So don't be mad when I say: <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393628531i/8742734._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>The ending of the book left us with a new heartbreak, and another cliffhanger in the form of a tidbit about Georgina's contract. Perhaps there is hope for our succubus after all. Another great book in the series; now only one to go.<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_85451732" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/85451732" />
    <a title="Shera (Book Whispers)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3167178-shera-book-whispers"><img alt="Shera (Book Whispers)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1446841556p2/3167178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/85451732?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shera (Book Whispers)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shera (Book Whispers)" href="/user/show/3167178-shera-book-whispers">Shera (Book Whispers)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3167178-shera-book-whispers?shelf=ebook-second">ebook-second</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3167178-shera-book-whispers?shelf=ebook-m">ebook-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3167178-shera-book-whispers?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3167178-shera-book-whispers?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3167178-shera-book-whispers?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3167178-shera-book-whispers?shelf=2010">2010</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer85451732" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5948729775096862270">Thoughts:<br/> <br/>Is it me, or does Georgina get whiter and whiter with these covers. No, I'm not talking pale. White. As in clown white. Scratch that, this is mime white, I feel like she's going to put her hands up to imaginary glass and do that creepy thing mimes do.<br/><br/>The covers may be degenerating over time, but Succubus Shadows picked up nicely from the last one. After the affair, I wasn't sure how Mead would make me get sucked back in. She did though, and this is the big turning point in the series. </span>
  <span id="freeText5948729775096862270" style="display:none">Thoughts:<br /> <br />Is it me, or does Georgina get whiter and whiter with these covers. No, I'm not talking pale. White. As in clown white. Scratch that, this is mime white, I feel like she's going to put her hands up to imaginary glass and do that creepy thing mimes do.<br /><br />The covers may be degenerating over time, but Succubus Shadows picked up nicely from the last one. After the affair, I wasn't sure how Mead would make me get sucked back in. She did though, and this is the big turning point in the series. That's right, the turning point, even more then the HUGE breakup(s).<br /><br />Crazy entities are still after Georgina, this time she's wondering why. Things are interested in her—her and Seth, more questions are being raised(at last) and some answers given. Even if Georgina isn't grasping a couple of them just yet. <br /><br />Georgina's love life is still in crisis. Roman's not out to kill her, he wants her back, and she's not sure where she stands with him. Seth is going forward with the wedding, and Georgina keeps getting pulled into the plans. She can't move on and blue moods persist, and things are preying on those moods promising her things she desperately needs right now. When she finally is sucked in, a new succubus is trying to bag and tag Seth pretending to be her. <br /><br />When she gives into it at last, dreams of truth and lies onslaught her as some of Nyx's children are out for revenge. All of those dreams could have turned into a tiring page after page dream sequence, but Mead knows what she's doing. She takes readers to some important truths from her past, and gives the readers some answers to Seth and Georgina's more-then-meets-the-eye relationship. Some of the present lies where really interesting to watch, and the present truths, watching how Roman is set out to find her was great. They all balanced so well. So why we are trapped in dream land, the reader can still see the rescue unfold. <br /><br />Roman developed a lot. So much so, I'm even more in love with him before. It hurt watching how much he went through to find Georgina and that he could let her go, because he could see where her heart was. Roman is one character I need to know where he is going to end up, it's now turned into an obsession for me.<br /><br />This was a character development book. Georgina past was so great to explore, learning how time took it's tole on her hellish role. Georgina grew up a lot, and I loved watching it. Other peeks at lives and interactions were great for the other characters. Seth has changed a lot, in part because Georgina came in to his life, but these are steps he took. Even after Georgian was “not” a part of it, he continued to change, but those are his choices. <br /><br />The drama cranks up at the end of Succubus Shadows, the dream man is revealed. And so much more, but I don't want to give it away. I did feel Georgina recovered a little too fast after her torture, this wasn't torture a strong person could have walked away from. I love Georgina, but she's not that strong.<br /><br />Bottom Line:<br /><br /> This may not be one of the biggest plot bombshell in the series, but this is a huge turning point. This book is also the one for character development, every one grows. The reader loves the characters more and everything is starting to lead up to the why of Georgina and Seth's love. This book fuels my Roman addiction and pulls off what could have been a tiring tell of dreams and more dreams. In the end all I can say is, “Go Mead, go Mead!” (Picture really stupid cheering moves.)<br /><br />Sexual Content:<br /> <br /> Yes, it did seem to be a little more toned down after the last one. This is still a Succubus book, look out.<br /><br />Rating: <br />5/5 – Ah, this is Heaven! Skipping this book is not an option.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5948729775096862270" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_70574804" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/70574804" />
    <a title="Mel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2295424-mel"><img alt="Mel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1305638929p2/2295424.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/70574804?book_show_action=true">Sep 09, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mel" href="/user/show/2295424-mel">Mel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780553820317" href="/book/show/7663247-succubus-shadows">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer70574804" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13092296696769477983">When I started out reading this series I really loved Georgina. I'm not quite sure how I feel about her now… <br/>Because eventhough Georgina seems very altruistic and angelic for a hellish creature, she is actually quite self centered. It's all about her. Always. Plus, she’s got the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/series/40628-the-hollows' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rachel Morgan</a> "woe is me, but in the mean time I’m the hottest thing on earth"- vibe going on. <br/>Mead has a way of making her characters seem ir-re-sis-ti-ble to everyone. Same with Eugenie from Thorn Queen. Everybody <i>love</i></span>
  <span id="freeText13092296696769477983" style="display:none">When I started out reading this series I really loved Georgina. I'm not quite sure how I feel about her now… <br />Because eventhough Georgina seems very altruistic and angelic for a hellish creature, she is actually quite self centered. It's all about her. Always. Plus, she’s got the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/40628-the-hollows" rel="nofollow noopener">Rachel Morgan</a> "woe is me, but in the mean time I’m the hottest thing on earth"- vibe going on. <br />Mead has a way of making her characters seem ir-re-sis-ti-ble to everyone. Same with Eugenie from Thorn Queen. Everybody <i>loves</i> and <i>adores</i> her, she is great in every way possible. It's too much. It gets annoying! <br />Sure, Seth has some sort of cosmic attraction to her but what about Roman? Why is he still in love? And more importantly: who died and made him a total whimp?!?<br /><br />Anyway, when I don't <i>really</i> like the character, I can't invest in anything that happens to them. The fact that half of the book felt like fillers to me (as we got told about a lot of stuff, but not live them) didn’t help much either. <br />Plus Mead has a way of spelling out the obvious. Circles, destiny, fate, “if it wasn’t for me”…. we get it! No need to repeat the same thing twenty times!<br />The story ends in a cliffhanger-fashion which would have actually been exciting if we hadn’t seen it all coming about two books ago. <br /><br />That being said: the book wasn’t bad. It was repetitive and almost boring at times but it wasn’t badly written and some parts were engaging and funny.<br /><br />I’m going to read the last one in the series as I would like to know how it all ends, but I won’t be running to the store. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13092296696769477983" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer513990638229476355">This book was freaking awesome. I loved it. Couldn't put it down, not for a single second.<br/><br/>I must say again that the world Richelle Mead has created is different from everything out there, so original. <br/><br/>I know it's weird but I think that what makes this series so amazing is Georgina. I just love to see a sex demon so concern about doing good to others and having so much happening to her. I love that the most moral person in the series is the one who shouldn't be. I think Georgina is one of the mos</span>
  <span id="freeText513990638229476355" style="display:none">This book was freaking awesome. I loved it. Couldn't put it down, not for a single second.<br /><br />I must say again that the world Richelle Mead has created is different from everything out there, so original. <br /><br />I know it's weird but I think that what makes this series so amazing is Georgina. I just love to see a sex demon so concern about doing good to others and having so much happening to her. I love that the most moral person in the series is the one who shouldn't be. I think Georgina is one of the most interesting characters I have found. Even without the rest of the story going on, Georgie would make me want to read the book. She has so many facets, and is such a complex character that you can't help to wanna know more about her. <br /><br />I think that a lot happens in this book. I loved the previous 2 books so much that I even added them to my favs shelf, but this one was way better. With books 3 and 4, even though I loved them, there were things in it that I didn't want them to happen.But this one was just perfect, I think that finally things are going the way they are supposed to be. I loved this book so much that I even added it to my 6 stars shelf. I don't wanna say more because I won't be able to stop saying things I should't and I don't wanna write any spoilers.<br /><br />Then there was the ending. WTF???!!! How am I suppose to wait a year to know what will happen? Although I think we knew it since they met. Saying he called her Letha makes it kinda obvious. OMG, can't wait for next book!<br /><br /><br />So, to sum up, this is a terrific series, one that you won't be able to stop with once you start it. <br /></span>

<div id="review_2031239740" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2031239740" />
    <a title="Deborah Obida" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/54790180-deborah-obida"><img alt="Deborah Obida" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604679377p2/54790180.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2031239740?book_show_action=true">Sep 12, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Deborah Obida" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Deborah Obida" href="/user/show/54790180-deborah-obida">Deborah Obida</a>
      </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('CSYjT6H7CrfZuQF6WTwbPGXs6YJcgLxVbqBPcsVhqMQzAEqdGqXD336StRuuyRHjs7MOSpINMjI13gnDCCJaXg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('1zUIybOB4x6fKEO4CNhUg0tMInQKRqJ/rQPlki7seN/tE2EbCN8qdjgD99n/LV5cnRPFvMTLLBj2faMj46+KRQ==')})
  }
//]]>

<span id="freeTextContainer15968206183132439387">Scorpio Richelle Mead is a New York Times and USA Today bestselling author of urban fantasy books for both adults and teens. Originally from Michigan, Richelle now lives in Seattle, Washington where she works on her three series full-time: Georgina Kincaid, Dark Swan, and Vampire Academy.<br/><br/>A life-long reader, Richelle has always loved mythology and folklore. When she can actually tear herself away f</span>
  <span id="freeText15968206183132439387" style="display:none">Scorpio Richelle Mead is a New York Times and USA Today bestselling author of urban fantasy books for both adults and teens. Originally from Michigan, Richelle now lives in Seattle, Washington where she works on her three series full-time: Georgina Kincaid, Dark Swan, and Vampire Academy.<br /><br />A life-long reader, Richelle has always loved mythology and folklore. When she can actually tear herself away from books (either reading or writing them), she enjoys bad reality TV, traveling, trying interesting cocktails, and shopping for dresses. She's a self-professed coffee addict and has a passion for all things wacky and humorous.<br /></span>
